FOR THE YEAR 1951 -1952 
First Sem ester 
Sept. 10, 11 and 12 ................................................. Registration with the Director of (Mon. , Tues. , Wed. ) Student Accounts and with the Deans for courses in the first sem ester. 
Sept. 13th (Thurs.) ............................................. Classes begin at 8:00 a.m . 
Sept. 16th (Sun. ).................................................. Form al opening the schoolyear with Solemn Mass and serm on by the President. 
Sept. 17th (Mon.)......................................................Latest date for essential class changes. 
Oct. 13th (Sat.) ......................................................Founder's Day (no classes.) 
Nov. 1st ( Thurs. )...............................................All Saints Day (no classes. ) 
Nov. 14th (W ed.) .............................................Midsem ester reports of deficient students. 
Nov. 15 to 21st..........................................................Preregistration with the Deans for courses for the second sem ester of 1951-52. (See Academic Regulation 113, General Bulletin.) 
Nov. 22nd (Thurs.) .............................................Thanksgiving Day (No classes). 
December 8th (Sat.) ......................................... Feast of the Immaculate Conception (no classes). 
Dec. 15th (Sat. ) ................................................. Latest date for comprehensive exami­nations, and dissertations of under­graduates. 
Dec. 20th (Thurs.) .................................................First day of Christm as vacation (no classes). 
Jan. 3rd (Thurs.) ................................................. Classes resum ed at 8:00 a.m . 
Jan. 17 to 24th ..................................................Sem ester examinations in all courses. (Thurs. to Thurs.) 
Second Sem ester Jan. 29, 30 th ..........................................................Registration with the Director of

RESIDENCE HALL PHONES 
RESIDENCE 


The purpose of the hall extension phones is for the reception of necessary long distance calls to students from family and friends. In order to keep trunk lines open, the operators on the Notre Dame switchboard have been instructed not to put through any local calls on hall extension phones. Instruct your friends locally to call the pay phone number in your hall. Please answer the phones for students' use in your hall. You do your fellow student a service.

Explanation of the code which follows the student's name in parentheses. 
The letter and number which follow each student's name m parentheses are to be indicated according to the following code. The letter desig ­nates the college, and the number indicates the class; for example, Smith, John J., (E-l) indicates Engineering, freshm an.
